Here's a summary of what was added:\n\n**`escape_with_encoding(text, encoding=\"utf-8\", strings_only=False, errors=\"strict\")`** in `django/utils/html.py`:\n\n1. **Protected types**: When `strings_only=True` and `text` is a protected type (int, float, Decimal, datetime, etc. as defined in `encoding.py`), returns the value as-is — matching the existing `force_str` behavior.\n\n2. **String conversion**: Uses `force_str()` with the specified `encoding` and `errors` to convert byte strings (or any other input) to a Python string. The `strings_only=False` is passed to `force_str` here because the protected type check was already done above.\n\n3. **HTML escaping**: Calls `conditional_escape()` which:\n   - Forces lazy translation objects (`Promise`) to evaluate\n   - Returns pre-escaped safe strings unchanged (via `__html__()`)\n   - HTML-escapes all other strings\n\n4. **Lazy imports**: Uses a local import of `force_str` and `is_protected_type` from `django.utils.encoding` to avoid any potential circular import issues (consistent with other deferred imports in the file like `DjangoJSONEncoder`)."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":360,"cache_read_input_tokens":46640,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":360,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7193d453-6ae4-4484-9811-083a9739c298","uuid":"745279b6-1214-4c09-af10-20b274cb77bc"}
